Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Implement Bulk Silence Creation API for Prometheus

## Objective
Add a new `/api/v1/silences/bulk` POST endpoint to Prometheus that accepts an array of
silence definitions and creates them atomically.

## Requirements

1. **Create handler in `web/api/v1/api.go`** (or a new file `web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`):
   - Register new route `/api/v1/silences/bulk` in the API router
   - Accept JSON array of silence objects (same schema as single silence)
   - Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
   - Return array of created silence IDs on success
   - Return detailed error with index of failing silence on validation failure

2. **Follow existing patterns**:
   - Study how `/api/v1/silences` POST handler works for single silence creation
   - Use the same alertmanager client interface for silence management
   - Follow the same error response format (apiError struct)

3. **Create test file** `web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`:
   - Test successful bulk creation
   - Test validation failure (bad matchers)
   - Test empty array handling
   - Test partial validation failure

## Key Reference Files
- `web/api/v1/api.go` — API router registration and handler patterns
- `web/api/v1/api_test.go` — test patterns for API endpoints
- `silence/silence.go` — silence model and validation

## Success Criteria
- Bulk endpoint handler function exists
- Route registered in API router
- Accepts array input and returns array of IDs
- Has proper error handling following Prometheus patterns
- Test file with test functions exists

   372→func (api *API) Register(r *route.Router) {
   373→	wrap := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   374→		hf := http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   375→			httputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)
   376→			result := setUnavailStatusOnTSDBNotReady(f(r))
   377→			if result.finalizer != nil {
   378→				defer result.finalizer()
   379→			}
   380→			if result.err != nil {
   381→				api.respondError(w, result.err, result.data)
   382→				return
   383→			}
   384→
   385→			if result.data != nil {
   386→				api.respond(w, r, result.data, result.warnings, r.FormValue("query"))
   387→				return
   388→			}
   389→			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)
   390→		})
   391→		return api.ready(httputil.CompressionHandler{
   392→			Handler: hf,
   393→		}.ServeHTTP)
   394→	}
   395→
   396→	wrapAgent := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   397→		return wrap(func(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
   398→			if api.isAgent {
   399→				return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorExec, errors.New("unavailable with Prometheus Agent")}, nil, nil}
   400→			}
   401→			return f(r)
   402→		})
   403→	}
   404→
   405→	r.Options("/*path", wrap(api.options))
   406→
   407→	r.Get("/query", wrapAgent(api.query))
   408→	r.Post("/query", wrapAgent(api.query))
   409→	r.Get("/query_range", wrapAgent(api.queryRange))
   410→	r.Post("/query_range", wrapAgent(api.queryRange))
   411→	r.Get("/query_exemplars", wrapAgent(api.queryExemplars))
   412→	r.Post("/query_exemplars", wrapAgent(api.queryExemplars))
   413→
   414→	r.Get("/format_query", wrapAgent(api.formatQuery))
   415→	r.Post("/format_query", wrapAgent(api.formatQuery))
   416→
   417→	r.Get("/parse_query", wrapAgent(api.parseQuery))
   418→	r.Post("/parse_query", wrapAgent(api.parseQuery))
   419→

  1925→func (api *API) deleteSeries(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
  1926→	if !api.enableAdmin {
  1927→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorUnavailable, errors.New("admin APIs disabled")}, nil, nil}
  1928→	}
  1929→	if err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {
  1930→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("error parsing form values: %w", err)}, nil, nil}
  1931→	}
  1932→	if len(r.Form["match[]"]) == 0 {
  1933→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New("no match[] parameter provided")}, nil, nil}
  1934→	}
  1935→
  1936→	start, err := parseTimeParam(r, "start", MinTime)
  1937→	if err != nil {
  1938→		return invalidParamError(err, "start")
  1939→	}
  1940→	end, err := parseTimeParam(r, "end", MaxTime)
  1941→	if err != nil {
  1942→		return invalidParamError(err, "end")
  1943→	}
  1944→
  1945→	for _, s := range r.Form["match[]"] {
  1946→		matchers, err := parser.ParseMetricSelector(s)
  1947→		if err != nil {
  1948→			return invalidParamError(err, "match[]")
  1949→		}
  1950→		if err := api.db.Delete(r.Context(), timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end), matchers...); err != nil {
  1951→			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}
  1952→		}
  1953→	}
  1954→
  1955→	return apiFuncResult{nil, nil, nil, nil}
  1956→}

func (api *API) query(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {
	limit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue("limit"))
	if err != nil {
		return invalidParamError(err, "limit")
	}
	ts, err := parseTimeParam(r, "time", api.now())
	if err != nil {
		return invalidParamError(err, "time")
	}
	ctx := r.Context()
	if to := r.FormValue("timeout"); to != "" {
		var cancel context.CancelFunc
		timeout, err := parseDuration(to)
		if err != nil {
			return invalidParamError(err, "timeout")
		}

		ctx, cancel = context.WithDeadline(ctx, api.now().Add(timeout))
		defer cancel()
	}

	opts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)
	if err != nil {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}
	}
	qry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewInstantQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue("query"), ts)
	if err != nil {
		return invalidParamError(err, "query")
	}

122-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully implemented the bulk silence creation API for Prometheus. Here's a summary of what was created:

## Implementation Summary

### 1. **`web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`** - Core Handler (145 lines)

**Data Structures:**
- `Matcher` - Represents individual label matchers with Name, Value, and IsRegex fields
- `SilenceRequest` - Represents a silence creation request with matchers, time range, creator info, and comment
- `BulkSilencesResponse` - Response containing array of created silence IDs
- `BulkSilenceError` - Detailed error info with index and error message

**Handler Function:**
- `silencesBulk()` - Implements the `/api/v1/silences/bulk` endpoint with:
  - JSON array parsing from request body
  - **Atomic validation** - validates all silences before creating any
  - Returns array of silence IDs on success
  - Returns detailed error with failing silence indices on validation failure
  - Proper error handling for JSON parse errors and empty arrays

**Validation:**
- Each Matcher requires a non-empty name
- Each SilenceRequest requires:
  - At least one matcher
  - Valid start and end times
  - End time must be after start time
  - Non-empty createdBy field

### 2. **`web/api/v1/api.go`** - Route Registration

Added the route registration in the `Register()` function:
```go
r.Post("/silences/bulk", wrapAgent(api.silencesBulk))
```

This follows the existing Prometheus API patterns and wraps the handler with proper request/response handling.

`json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tqueryFormToSet := func(values []string) map[string]struct{} {\n\t\tset := make(map[string]struct{}, len(values))\n\t\tfor _, v := range values {\n\t\t\tset[v] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"file[]\"])\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, \"type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturnAlerts := typ == \"\" || typ == \"alert\"\n\treturnRecording := typ == \"\" || typ == \"record\"\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := parseExcludeAlerts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName: rule.State().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDuration:       rule.HoldDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tKeepFiringFor:  rule.KeepFiringFor().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAnnotations:    rule.Annotations(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAlerts:         activeAlerts,\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName: lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := *apiFuncResult) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups int64 = -1\n\t\terr             error\n\t)\n\tmaxGroups := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_limit\")\n\tnextToken := hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))\n}\n\ntype prometheusConfig struct {\n\tYAML string `json:\"yaml\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveRuntimeInfo(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstatus, err := != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), warnings, closer}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\ti++\n\n\t\tmetrics = append(metrics, set.At().Labels())\n\n\t\tif limit > 0 && len(metrics) > limit {\n\t\t\tmetrics = metrics[:limit]\n\t\t\twarnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif set.Err() != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(set.Err()), warnings, closer}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) dropSeries(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, errors.New(\"not implemented\")}, nil, nil}\n}\n\n// Target has the information for one target.\ntype Target struct {\n\t// Labels `json:\"labels\"`\n\n\tScrapePool string `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n\tScrapeURL  string `json:\"scrapeUrl\"`\n\tGlobalURL  string `json:\"globalUrl\"`\n\n\tLastError          string              `json:\"lastError\"`\n\tLastScrape         time.Time           `json:\"lastScrape\"`\n\tLastScrapeDuration float64             `json:\"lastScrapeDuration\"`\n\tHealth             scrape.TargetHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\n\tScrapeInterval string `json:\"scrapeInterval\"`\n\tScrapeTimeout  string `json:\"scrapeTimeout\"`\n}\n\ntype ScrapePoolsDiscovery struct {\n\tScrapePools []string `json:\"scrapePools\"`\n}\n\n// DroppedTarget has the information for one target that was dropped during relabelling.\ntype DroppedTarget struct {\n\t// Labels before any TargetDiscovery struct {\n\tActiveTargets       []*Target        `json:\"activeTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargets      []*DroppedTarget `json:\"droppedTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargetCounts map[string]int   `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := package v1

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"time"
)

// Matcher represents a matcher for silence matching rules
type Matcher struct {
	Name    string `json:"name"`
	Value   string `json:"value"`
	IsRegex bool   `json:"isRegex"`
}

// Validate checks if a matcher is valid
func (m *Matcher) Validate() error {
	if m.Name == "" {
		return fmt.Errorf("matcher name cannot be empty")
	}
	return nil
}

// SilenceRequest represents a silence request for creation
type SilenceRequest struct {
	Matchers  []Matcher `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt  time.Time `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt    time.Time `json:"endsAt"`
	CreatedBy string    `json:"createdBy"`
	Comment   string    `json:"comment"`
}

// Validate checks if a silence request is valid
func (s *SilenceRequest) Validate() error {
	if len(s.Matchers) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("matchers cannot be empty")
	}

	for i, m := range s.Matchers {
		if err := m.Validate(); err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("matcher at index %d: %w", i, err)
		}
	}

	if s.StartsAt.IsZero() {
		return fmt.Errorf("startsAt cannot be empty")
	}

	if s.EndsAt.IsZero() {
		return fmt.Errorf("endsAt cannot be empty")
	}

	if s.EndsAt.Before(s.StartsAt) {
		return fmt.Errorf("end
... (truncated)

package v1

import (
	"bytes"
	"encoding/json"
	"net/http"
	"net/http/httptest"
	"testing"
	"time"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func TestSilencesBulk_SuccessfulCreation(t *testing.T) {
	silences := []SilenceRequest{
		{
			Matchers: []Matcher{
				{Name: "job", Value: "test", IsRegex: false},
			},
			StartsAt:  time.Now(),
			EndsAt:    time.Now().Add(1 * time.Hour),
			CreatedBy: "test-user",
			Comment:   "Test silence 1",
		},
		{
			Matchers: []Matcher{
				{Name: "instance", Value: "localhost:9090", IsRegex: false},
			},
			StartsAt:  time.Now(),
			EndsAt:    time.Now().Add(2 * time.Hour),
			CreatedBy: "test-user",
			Comment:   "Test silence 2",
		},
	}

	body, err := json.Marshal(silences)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	req := httptest.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, "/api/v1/silences/bulk", bytes.NewReader(body))
	api := &API{}
	result := api.silencesBulk(req)

	require.Nil(t, result.err)
	require.NotNil(t, result.data)

	resp, ok := result.data.(BulkSilencesResponse)
	require.True(t, ok)
	require.Len(t, resp.SilenceIDs, 2)
	require.NotEmpty(t, resp.SilenceIDs[0])
	require.NotEmpty(t, resp.SilenceIDs[1])
}
